 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-01-31' AND Hour = 20) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-01-31' AND Hour = 20) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  20 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 20) tt2,

 			SELECT * FROM `winddb` 
			GROUP BY `Date`
			ORDER BY Date ASC
 		
 			SELECT * FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date` = (SELECT MIN(Date) FROM `winddb`)
 		
 			SELECT * FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1
 		
 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-01-31' AND Hour = 22) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-01-31' AND Hour = 22) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  22 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 22 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 22 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 22 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 22) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt
 		
 			SELECT * FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date` = '2019-01-31'

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM

			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 22 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 22) tt2,

			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

`shifted_energydb` WHERE  `actual_hour` = 23 AND `sender` = 'F'SELECT IFNULL(SUM(`shifted_energy`),0) AS shifted_energy  FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE  `shifted_hour` = 23 AND `sender` = 'F'
			SELECT 
				hour,
			    MAX(`energy`) AS peak_energy,
			    ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) AS avg_engery
			    
			FROM
				 householddb 
		
			SELECT 			db.*
			FROM
				 		   householddb db 
            INNER JOIN     dynamic_pricing dp
            ON dp.hour = db.hour
			WHERE db.energy < (SELECT
			    				ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) 
							FROM
			    				householddb 
			               )
			ORDER BY dp.price ASC
		
			SELECT * 
			FROM `shifted_energydb` 
			WHERE `shifted_hour` =5 
			AND `actual_hour` = 0
			AND `sender` = 'H'
		
				INSERT INTO `shifted_energydb` (`shifted_hour`, `shifted_energy`, `actual_hour`, `sender`)
				VALUES ( '5', '0.1204', '0', 'H')
			SELECT * 
			FROM `shifted_energydb` 
			WHERE `shifted_hour` =4

			SELECT 
				hour,
			    MAX(`energy`) AS peak_energy,
			    ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) AS avg_engery
			    
			FROM
				 commercialdb 
		
			SELECT 			db.*
			FROM
				 		   commercialdb db 
            INNER JOIN     dynamic_pricing dp
            ON dp.hour = db.hour
			WHERE db.energy < (SELECT
			    				ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) 
							FROM
			    				commercialdb 
			               )
			ORDER BY dp.price ASC
		
			SELECT * 
			FROM `shifted_energydb` 
			WHERE `shifted_hour` =5 
			AND `actual_hour` = 0
			AND `sender` = 'F'
		
				UPDATE `shifted_energydb` 
				SET `shifted_energy` = 41.7577
				WHERE `shifted_hour` =5 
				AND `actual_hour` = 0
				AND `sender` = 'F'

 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-01' AND Hour = 21) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-01' AND Hour = 21) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  21 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 21 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 21 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 21 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 21) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 19) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 19) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  19 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 19) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 19) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 19) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  19 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 19) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 19) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 19) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  19 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 19 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 19) tt2,

			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM

			SELECT 
				hour,
			    MAX(`energy`) AS peak_energy,
			    ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) AS avg_engery
			    
			FROM
				 commercialdb 
		
			SELECT 			db.*
			FROM
				 		   commercialdb db 
            INNER JOIN     dynamic_pricing dp
            ON dp.hour = db.hour
			WHERE db.energy < (SELECT
			    				ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) 
							FROM
			    				commercialdb 
			               )
			ORDER BY dp.price ASC

 			SELECT * FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1
 		
 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 20) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 20) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  20 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 20) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

 			SELECT * FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1
 		
 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 20) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-04' AND Hour = 20) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  20 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 20) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  20 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 20 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 20) tt2,

			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt

			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  10 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 10) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt
 		
 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-08' AND Hour = 10) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-08' AND Hour = 10) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT * FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1

				hour,
			    MAX(`energy`) AS peak_energy,

			SELECT 			db.*
			FROM
				 		   householddb db 
            INNER JOIN     dynamic_pricing dp
            ON dp.hour = db.hour
			WHERE db.energy < (SELECT
			    				ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) 
							FROM
			    				householddb 
			               )
			ORDER BY dp.price ASC

			SELECT 			db.*
			FROM
				 		   commercialdb db 
            INNER JOIN     dynamic_pricing dp
            ON dp.hour = db.hour
			WHERE db.energy < (SELECT
			    				ROUND(AVG(`energy`),4) 
							FROM
			    				commercialdb 
			               )
			ORDER BY dp.price ASC

 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-08' AND Hour = 10) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-08' AND Hour = 10) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  10 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 10) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt
 		
 			SELECT * FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date` = '2019-02-08'

 			SELECT * FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date` = '2019-02-08'
 		
 			SELECT * FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date` = '2019-02-09'
 		
 			SELECT tt1.shifted_energy + tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy - tt1.actual_energy AS total_demand, tt2.house_energy + tt2.commercial_energy + tt.avg_house_eng + tt.avg_commercial_eng AS max_demand   FROM

			(SELECT t1.shifted_energy + t3.shifted_energy AS shifted_energy, t2.shifted_energy + t4.shifted_energy AS actual_energy FROM 
			(SELECT  IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` =  10 AND `sender` = 'H') t1,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'H')t2,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `shifted_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'F') t3,
			(SELECT IFNULL(SUM(shifted_energy), 0) AS shifted_energy FROM `shifted_energydb` WHERE `actual_hour` = 10 AND `sender` = 'F')t4)tt1,

			(SELECT  h.energy AS house_energy, c.energy AS commercial_energy FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour AND c.hour = 10) tt2,

			(SELECT  AVG(h.energy) AS avg_house_eng, AVG(c.energy) AS avg_commercial_eng FROM householddb h, commercialdb c
			WHERE h.hour = c.hour)tt
 		
 			SELECT (t1.ProducedEnergy + t2.ProducedEnergy + t3.battery_storage) total_supply FROM
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `winddb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-08' AND Hour = 10) t1,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`ProducedEnergy`, 0) AS ProducedEnergy FROM `solardb` WHERE `Date`  = '2019-02-08' AND Hour = 10) t2,
				(SELECT IFNULL(`battery_storage`, 0) AS battery_storage FROM `setupdb` WHERE user_id = 1) t3
